```python
'''

Main entry point for the application.

def main():
    app = QApplication(sys.argv)
    window = MainWindow()
    window.show()

    main()
```

#### models.py

```python
'''

Django models for storing documents and formulas.

'''

from django.db import models

class Document(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()

class Formula(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    expression = models.TextField()
```

#### nlp_utils.py

```python
'''

NLP utilities for text summarization.

'''

import spacy

nlp = spacy.load("en_core_web_sm")

def summarize_text(text):
    # Simple summarization logic
    doc = nlp(text)
    summary = ' '.join([sent.text for sent in doc.sents][:3])  # Example: first 3 sentences
    return summary
```

#### formula_utils.py

```python
'''

Utilities for formula evaluation.

'''

def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
    # Evaluate the formula using the provided variables
    try:
        result = eval(expression, {}, variables)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        return str(e)
```

#### gui.py

```python
'''

PyQt5 GUI implementation for the application.

'''

from PyQt5.QtWidgets import QMainWindow, QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QPushButton, QLabel, QFileDialog

class MainWindow(QMainWindow):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setWindowTitle("Document Summarizer and Formula Builder")
        self.setGeometry(100, 100, 800, 600)
        
        self.central_widget = QWidget()
        self.setCentralWidget(self.central_widget)
        
        self.layout = QVBoxLayout()
        self.central_widget.setLayout(self.layout)
        
        self.upload_button = QPushButton("Upload Documents")
        self.upload_button.clicked.connect(self.upload_documents)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.upload_button)
        
        self.summary_label = QLabel("Summary will appear here.")
        self.layout.addWidget(self.summary_label)
        
        self.formula_button = QPushButton("Evaluate Formula")
        self.formula_button.clicked.connect(self.evaluate_formula)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.formula_button)
        
    def upload_documents(self):
        # Logic to handle document upload
        file_dialog = QFileDialog()
        file_dialog.setFileMode(QFileDialog.ExistingFiles)
        file_dialog.setNameFilter("Text files (*.txt)")
        if file_dialog.exec_():
            file_names = file_dialog.selectedFiles()
            # Process files
            self.summary_label.setText("Documents uploaded.")
        
    def evaluate_formula(self):
        # Logic to evaluate a formula
        self.summary_label.setText("Formula evaluated.")
```

This setup provides a basic structure for the application, integrating Django for backend processing, React for frontend interaction, and PyQt5 for a desktop GUI. Each component is designed to handle specific tasks, ensuring modularity and ease of maintenance.

```python
import spacy
nlp = spacy.load("en_core_web_sm")
def summarize_text(text):
    # Simple summarization logic
    doc = nlp(text)
    summary = ' '.join([sent.text for sent in doc.sents][:3])  # Example: first 3 sentences
    return summary
```

```python
'''

def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
    # Evaluate the formula using the provided variables
    try:
        result = eval(expression, {}, variables)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        return str(e)
```

### views.py
```python
'''
Django views for handling document uploads and formula operations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt
from .models import Document, Formula
from .nlp_utils import summarize_text
from .formula_utils import evaluate_formula
import json

@csrf_exempt
def upload_documents(request):
    '''
    Handle document uploads and save them to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        files = request.FILES.getlist('documents')
        for file in files:
            content = file.read().decode('utf-8')
            Document.objects.create(title=file.name, content=content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Documents uploaded successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})

@csrf_exempt
def generate_summary(request, document_id):
    '''
    Generate a summary for a specific document.
    '''
    try:
        document = Document.objects.get(id=document_id)
        summary = summarize_text(document.content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'summary': summary})
    except Document.DoesNotExist:
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Document not found.'})

@csrf_exempt
def save_formula(request):
    '''
    Save a new formula to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        name = data.get('name')
        expression = data.get('expression')
        Formula.objects.create(name=name, expression=expression)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Formula saved successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})

@csrf_exempt
def evaluate_formula_view(request):
    '''
    Evaluate a formula using provided variables.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        formula_id = data.get('formula_id')
        variables = data.get('variables', {})
        try:
            formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id)
            result = evaluate_formula(formula.expression, variables)
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'result': result})
        except Formula.DoesNotExist:
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Formula not found.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
```

### views.py
```python
'''
Django views for handling document uploads and formula operations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt
from .models import Document, Formula
from .nlp_utils import summarize_text
from .formula_utils import evaluate_formula
import json

@csrf_exempt
def upload_documents(request):
    '''
    Handle document uploads and save them to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        files = request.FILES.getlist('documents')
        for file in files:
            content = file.read().decode('utf-8')
            Document.objects.create(title=file.name, content=content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Documents uploaded successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})

@csrf_exempt
def generate_summary(request, document_id):
    '''
    Generate a summary for a specific document.
    '''
    try:
        document = Document.objects.get(id=document_id)
        summary = summarize_text(document.content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'summary': summary})
    except Document.DoesNotExist:
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Document not found.'})

@csrf_exempt
def save_formula(request):
    '''
    Save a new formula to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        name = data.get('name')
        expression = data.get('expression')
        Formula.objects.create(name=name, expression=expression)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Formula saved successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})

@csrf_exempt
def evaluate_formula_view(request):
    '''
    Evaluate a formula using provided variables.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        formula_id = data.get('formula_id')
        variables = data.get('variables', {})
        try:
            formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id)
            result = evaluate_formula(formula.expression, variables)
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'result': result})
        except Formula.DoesNotExist:
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Formula not found.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
```

```python
'''
```
```python
Main entry point for the application.
'''
from gui import MainWindow
from PyQt5.QtWidgets import QApplication
import sys
def main():
    app = QApplication(sys.argv)
    window = MainWindow()
    window.show()
    sys.exit(app.exec_())
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

views.py
```python
'''
Django views for handling document uploads and formula operations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt
from .models import Document, Formula
from .nlp_utils import summarize_text
from .formula_utils import evaluate_formula
import json
@csrf_exempt
def upload_documents(request):
    '''
    Handle document uploads and save them to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        files = request.FILES.getlist('documents')
        for file in files:
            content = file.read().decode('utf-8')
            Document.objects.create(title=file.name, content=content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Documents uploaded successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def generate_summary(request, document_id):
    '''
    Generate a summary for a specific document.
    '''
    try:
        document = Document.objects.get(id=document_id)
        summary = summarize_text(document.content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'summary': summary})
    except Document.DoesNotExist:
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Document not found.'})
@csrf_exempt
def save_formula(request):
    '''
    Save a new formula to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        name = data.get('name')
        expression = data.get('expression')
        Formula.objects.create(name=name, expression=expression)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Formula saved successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def evaluate_formula_view(request):
    '''
    Evaluate a formula using provided variables.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        formula_id = data.get('formula_id')
        variables = data.get('variables', {})
        try:
            formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id)
            result = evaluate_formula(formula.expression, variables)
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'result': result})
        except Formula.DoesNotExist:
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Formula not found.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Django models for storing documents and formulas.
'''
from django.db import models
class Document(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()
class Formula(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    expression = models.TextField()
```

nlp_utils.py
```python
'''
NLP utilities for text summarization.
'''
import spacy
nlp = spacy.load("en_core_web_sm")
def summarize_text(text):
    '''
    Simple summarization logic.
    '''
    doc = nlp(text)
    summary = ' '.join([sent.text for sent in doc.sents][:3])  # Example: first 3 sentences
    return summary
```

formula_utils.py
```python
'''
Utilities for formula evaluation.
'''
def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
    '''
    Evaluate the formula using the provided variables.
    '''
    try:
        result = eval(expression, {}, variables)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        return str(e)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
PyQt5 GUI implementation for the application.
'''
from PyQt5.QtWidgets import QMainWindow, QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QPushButton, QLabel, QFileDialog
class MainWindow(QMainWindow):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setWindowTitle("Document Summarizer and Formula Builder")
        self.setGeometry(100, 100, 800, 600)
        self.central_widget = QWidget()
        self.setCentralWidget(self.central_widget)
        self.layout = QVBoxLayout()
        self.central_widget.setLayout(self.layout)
        self.upload_button = QPushButton("Upload Documents")
        self.upload_button.clicked.connect(self.upload_documents)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.upload_button)
        self.summary_label = QLabel("Summary will appear here.")
        self.layout.addWidget(self.summary_label)
        self.formula_button = QPushButton("Evaluate Formula")
        self.formula_button.clicked.connect(self.evaluate_formula)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.formula_button)
    def upload_documents(self):
        '''
        Logic to handle document upload.
        '''
        file_dialog = QFileDialog()
        file_dialog.setFileMode(QFileDialog.ExistingFiles)
        file_dialog.setNameFilter("Text files (*.txt)")
        if file_dialog.exec_():
            file_names = file_dialog.selectedFiles()
            # Process files
            self.summary_label.setText("Documents uploaded.")
    def evaluate_formula(self):
        '''
        Logic to evaluate a formula.
        '''
        self.summary_label.setText("Formula evaluated.")
```

views.py
```python
'''
Django views for handling document uploads and formula operations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt
from .models import Document, Formula
from .nlp_utils import summarize_text
from .formula_utils import evaluate_formula
import json
@csrf_exempt
def upload_documents(request):
    '''
    Handle document uploads and save them to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        files = request.FILES.getlist('documents')
        for file in files:
            content = file.read().decode('utf-8')
            Document.objects.create(title=file.name, content=content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Documents uploaded successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def generate_summary(request, document_id):
    '''
    Generate a summary for a specific document.
    '''
    try:
        document = Document.objects.get(id=document_id)
        summary = summarize_text(document.content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'summary': summary})
    except Document.DoesNotExist:
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Document not found.'})
@csrf_exempt
def save_formula(request):
    '''
    Save a new formula to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        name = data.get('name')
        expression = data.get('expression')
        Formula.objects.create(name=name, expression=expression)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Formula saved successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def evaluate_formula_view(request):
    '''
    Evaluate a formula using provided variables.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        formula_id = data.get('formula_id')
        variables = data.get('variables', {})
        try:
            formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id)
            result = evaluate_formula(formula.expression, variables)
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'result': result})
        except Formula.DoesNotExist:
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Formula not found.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
```

```python
'''
Django models for storing documents and formulas.

from django.db import models
class Document(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()
class Formula(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    expression = models.TextField()
```

nlp_utils.py
```python
'''
NLP utilities for text summarization.
'''
import spacy
nlp = spacy.load("en_core_web_sm")
def summarize_text(text):
    '''
    Simple summarization logic.
    '''
    doc = nlp(text)
    summary = ' '.join([sent.text for sent in doc.sents][:3])  # Example: first 3 sentences
    return summary
```

formula_utils.py
```python
'''
Utilities for formula evaluation.
'''
def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
    '''
    Evaluate the formula using the provided variables.
    '''
    try:
        result = eval(expression, {}, variables)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        return str(e)
```

```python
from PyQt5.QtWidgets import QMainWindow, QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QPushButton, QLabel, QFileDialog
class MainWindow(QMainWindow):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setWindowTitle("Document Summarizer and Formula Builder")
        self.setGeometry(100, 100, 800, 600)
        self.central_widget = QWidget()
        self.setCentralWidget(self.central_widget)
        self.layout = QVBoxLayout()
        self.central_widget.setLayout(self.layout)
        self.upload_button = QPushButton("Upload Documents")
        self.upload_button.clicked.connect(self.upload_documents)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.upload_button)
        self.summary_label = QLabel("Summary will appear here.")
        self.layout.addWidget(self.summary_label)
        self.formula_button = QPushButton("Evaluate Formula")
        self.formula_button.clicked.connect(self.evaluate_formula)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.formula_button)
    def upload_documents(self):
        '''
        Logic to handle document upload.
        '''
        file_dialog = QFileDialog()
        file_dialog.setFileMode(QFileDialog.ExistingFiles)
        file_dialog.setNameFilter("Text files (*.txt)")
        if file_dialog.exec_():
            file_names = file_dialog.selectedFiles()
            # Process files
            self.summary_label.setText("Documents uploaded.")
    def evaluate_formula(self):
        '''
        Logic to evaluate a formula.
        '''
        self.summary_label.setText("Formula evaluated.")
```

```python
from .models import Document, Formula
from .nlp_utils import summarize_text
from .formula_utils import evaluate_formula

@csrf_exempt
def upload_documents(request):
    '''
    Handle document uploads and save them to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        files = request.FILES.getlist('documents')
        for file in files:
            content = file.read().decode('utf-8')
            Document.objects.create(title=file.name, content=content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Documents uploaded successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})

@csrf_exempt
def generate_summary(request, document_id):
    '''
    Generate a summary for a specific document.
    '''
    try:
        document = Document.objects.get(id=document_id)
        summary = summarize_text(document.content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'summary': summary})
    except Document.DoesNotExist:
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Document not found.'})

@csrf_exempt
def save_formula(request):
    '''
    Save a new formula to the database.

    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        name = data.get('name')
        expression = data.get('expression')
        Formula.objects.create(name=name, expression=expression)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Formula saved successfully.'})

    '''
    Evaluate a formula using provided variables.
    '''

        try:
            formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id)
```

```python
import spacy

nlp = spacy.load("en_core_web_sm")

def summarize_text(text):

    Simple summarization logic.

    doc = nlp(text)
```

```python
'''

def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
    '''
    Evaluate the formula using the provided variables.
    '''
    try:
        result = eval(expression, {}, variables)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        return str(e)
```

**Frontend (React or Vue.js):**

For the front end, you can choose either React or Vue.js. Below is a basic structure for a React application:

App.js
```javascript
'''
React component for the main application interface.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

function App() {
    const [documents, setDocuments] = useState([]);
    const [summary, setSummary] = useState('');
    const [formulaResult, setFormulaResult] = useState('');

    const uploadDocuments = async (event) => {
        const files = event.target.files;
        const formData = new FormData();
        for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
            formData.append('documents', files[i]);
        }
        const response = await axios.post('/upload_documents', formData);
        console.log(response.data.message);
    };

    const generateSummary = async (documentId) => {
        const response = await axios.get(`/generate_summary/${documentId}`);
        setSummary(response.data.summary);
    };

    const evaluateFormula = async (formulaId, variables) => {
        const response = await axios.post('/evaluate_formula_view', { formula_id: formulaId, variables });
        setFormulaResult(response.data.result);
    };

    return (
        <div>
            <h1>Document Summarizer and Formula Builder</h1>
            <input type="file" multiple onChange={uploadDocuments} />
            <button onClick={() => generateSummary(1)}>Generate Summary</button>
            <p>Summary: {summary}</p>
            <button onClick={() => evaluateFormula(1, { x: 10, y: 5 })}>Evaluate Formula</button>
            <p>Formula Result: {formulaResult}</p>
        </div>
    );
}

export default App;
```

This setup provides a basic structure for the React front end to interact with the Django backend. You can expand the front end with more features and styling as needed.

```python
'''
Main entry point for the Django application.
'''
import os
import sys
from django.core.wsgi import get_wsgi_application
os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'myproject.settings')
application = get_wsgi_application()
```

views.py
```python
'''
Django views for handling document uploads and formula operations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt
from .models import Document, Formula
from .nlp_utils import summarize_text
from .formula_utils import evaluate_formula
import json
@csrf_exempt
def upload_documents(request):
    '''
    Handle document uploads and save them to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        files = request.FILES.getlist('documents')
        for file in files:
            content = file.read().decode('utf-8')
            Document.objects.create(title=file.name, content=content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Documents uploaded successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def generate_summary(request, document_id):
    '''
    Generate a summary for a specific document.
    '''
    try:
        document = Document.objects.get(id=document_id)
        summary = summarize_text(document.content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'summary': summary})
    except Document.DoesNotExist:
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Document not found.'})
@csrf_exempt
def save_formula(request):
    '''
    Save a new formula to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        name = data.get('name')
        expression = data.get('expression')
        Formula.objects.create(name=name, expression=expression)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Formula saved successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def evaluate_formula_view(request):
    '''
    Evaluate a formula using provided variables.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        formula_id = data.get('formula_id')
        variables = data.get('variables', {})
        try:
            formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id)
            result = evaluate_formula(formula.expression, variables)
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'result': result})
        except Formula.DoesNotExist:
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Formula not found.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Django models for storing documents and formulas.
'''
from django.db import models
class Document(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()
class Formula(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    expression = models.TextField()
```

nlp_utils.py
```python
'''
NLP utilities for text summarization.
'''
import spacy
nlp = spacy.load("en_core_web_sm")
def summarize_text(text):
    '''
    Simple summarization logic.
    '''
    doc = nlp(text)
    summary = ' '.join([sent.text for sent in doc.sents][:3])  # Example: first 3 sentences
    return summary
```

formula_utils.py
```python
'''
Utilities for formula evaluation.
'''
def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
    '''
    Evaluate the formula using the provided variables.
    '''
    try:
        result = eval(expression, {}, variables)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        return str(e)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
PyQt5 GUI implementation for the application.
'''
from PyQt5.QtWidgets import QMainWindow, QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QPushButton, QLabel, QFileDialog
class MainWindow(QMainWindow):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setWindowTitle("Document Summarizer and Formula Builder")
        self.setGeometry(100, 100, 800, 600)
        self.central_widget = QWidget()
        self.setCentralWidget(self.central_widget)
        self.layout = QVBoxLayout()
        self.central_widget.setLayout(self.layout)
        self.upload_button = QPushButton("Upload Documents")
        self.upload_button.clicked.connect(self.upload_documents)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.upload_button)
        self.summary_label = QLabel("Summary will appear here.")
        self.layout.addWidget(self.summary_label)
        self.formula_button = QPushButton("Evaluate Formula")
        self.formula_button.clicked.connect(self.evaluate_formula)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.formula_button)
    def upload_documents(self):
        '''
        Logic to handle document upload.
        '''
        file_dialog = QFileDialog()
        file_dialog.setFileMode(QFileDialog.ExistingFiles)
        file_dialog.setNameFilter("Text files (*.txt)")
        if file_dialog.exec_():
            file_names = file_dialog.selectedFiles()
            # Process files
            self.summary_label.setText("Documents uploaded.")
    def evaluate_formula(self):
        '''
        Logic to evaluate a formula.
        '''
        self.summary_label.setText("Formula evaluated.")
```

app.js
```js
'''
React component for the main application interface.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function App() {
    const [documents, setDocuments] = useState([]);
    const [summary, setSummary] = useState('');
    const [formulaResult, setFormulaResult] = useState('');
    const uploadDocuments = async (event) => {
        const files = event.target.files;
        const formData = new FormData();
        for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
            formData.append('documents', files[i]);
        }
        const response = await axios.post('/upload_documents', formData);
        console.log(response.data.message);
    };
    const generateSummary = async (documentId) => {
        const response = await axios.get(`/generate_summary/${documentId}`);
        setSummary(response.data.summary);
    };
    const evaluateFormula = async (formulaId, variables) => {
        const response = await axios.post('/evaluate_formula_view', { formula_id: formulaId, variables });
        setFormulaResult(response.data.result);
    };
    return (
        <div>
            <h1>Document Summarizer and Formula Builder</h1>
            <input type="file" multiple onChange={uploadDocuments} />
            <button onClick={() => generateSummary(1)}>Generate Summary</button>
            <p>Summary: {summary}</p>
            <button onClick={() => evaluateFormula(1, { x: 10, y: 5 })}>Evaluate Formula</button>
            <p>Formula Result: {formulaResult}</p>
        </div>
    );
}
export default App;
```

Task: "Please help me implement a Python/Django or Node/Express web application with a React/Vue front end that enables bulk upload of documents, generates concise summaries using NLP, and includes a flexible formula builder for financial calculations, allowing users to save and edit formulas.".

"main.py
```python
'''
Main entry point for the Django application.
'''
import os
import sys
from django.core.wsgi import get_wsgi_application
os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'myproject.settings')
application = get_wsgi_application()
```

views.py
```python
'''
Django views for handling document uploads and formula operations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt
from .models import Document, Formula
from .nlp_utils import summarize_text
from .formula_utils import evaluate_formula
import json
@csrf_exempt
def upload_documents(request):
    '''
    Handle document uploads and save them to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        files = request.FILES.getlist('documents')
        for file in files:
            content = file.read().decode('utf-8')
            Document.objects.create(title=file.name, content=content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Documents uploaded successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def generate_summary(request, document_id):
    '''
    Generate a summary for a specific document.
    '''
    try:
        document = Document.objects.get(id=document_id)
        summary = summarize_text(document.content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'summary': summary})
    except Document.DoesNotExist:
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Document not found.'})
@csrf_exempt
def save_formula(request):
    '''
    Save a new formula to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        name = data.get('name')
        expression = data.get('expression')
        Formula.objects.create(name=name, expression=expression)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Formula saved successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def evaluate_formula_view(request):
    '''
    Evaluate a formula using provided variables.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        formula_id = data.get('formula_id')
        variables = data.get('variables', {})
        try:
            formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id)
            result = evaluate_formula(formula.expression, variables)
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'result': result})
        except Formula.DoesNotExist:
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Formula not found.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Django models for storing documents and formulas.
'''
from django.db import models
class Document(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()
class Formula(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    expression = models.TextField()
```

nlp_utils.py
```python
'''
NLP utilities for text summarization.
'''
import spacy
nlp = spacy.load("en_core_web_sm")
def summarize_text(text):
    '''
    Simple summarization logic.
    '''
    doc = nlp(text)
    summary = ' '.join([sent.text for sent in doc.sents][:3])  # Example: first 3 sentences
    return summary
```

formula_utils.py
```python
'''
Utilities for formula evaluation.
'''
def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
    '''
    Evaluate the formula using the provided variables.
    '''
    try:
        result = eval(expression, {}, variables)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        return str(e)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
PyQt5 GUI implementation for the application.
'''
from PyQt5.QtWidgets import QMainWindow, QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QPushButton, QLabel, QFileDialog
class MainWindow(QMainWindow):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setWindowTitle("Document Summarizer and Formula Builder")
        self.setGeometry(100, 100, 800, 600)
        self.central_widget = QWidget()
        self.setCentralWidget(self.central_widget)
        self.layout = QVBoxLayout()
        self.central_widget.setLayout(self.layout)
        self.upload_button = QPushButton("Upload Documents")
        self.upload_button.clicked.connect(self.upload_documents)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.upload_button)
        self.summary_label = QLabel("Summary will appear here.")
        self.layout.addWidget(self.summary_label)
        self.formula_button = QPushButton("Evaluate Formula")
        self.formula_button.clicked.connect(self.evaluate_formula)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.formula_button)
    def upload_documents(self):
        '''
        Logic to handle document upload.
        '''
        file_dialog = QFileDialog()
        file_dialog.setFileMode(QFileDialog.ExistingFiles)
        file_dialog.setNameFilter("Text files (*.txt)")
        if file_dialog.exec_():
            file_names = file_dialog.selectedFiles()
            # Process files
            self.summary_label.setText("Documents uploaded.")
    def evaluate_formula(self):
        '''
        Logic to evaluate a formula.
        '''
        self.summary_label.setText("Formula evaluated.")
```

app.js
```js
'''
React component for the main application interface.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function App() {
    const [documents, setDocuments] = useState([]);
    const [summary, setSummary] = useState('');
    const [formulaResult, setFormulaResult] = useState('');
    const uploadDocuments = async (event) => {
        const files = event.target.files;
        const formData = new FormData();
        for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
            formData.append('documents', files[i]);
        }
        const response = await axios.post('/upload_documents', formData);
        console.log(response.data.message);
    };
    const generateSummary = async (documentId) => {
        const response = await axios.get(`/generate_summary/${documentId}`);
        setSummary(response.data.summary);
    };
    const evaluateFormula = async (formulaId, variables) => {
        const response = await axios.post('/evaluate_formula_view', { formula_id: formulaId, variables });
        setFormulaResult(response.data.result);
    };
    return (
        <div>
            <h1>Document Summarizer and Formula Builder</h1>
            <input type="file" multiple onChange={uploadDocuments} />
            <button onClick={() => generateSummary(1)}>Generate Summary</button>
            <p>Summary: {summary}</p>
            <button onClick={() => evaluateFormula(1, { x: 10, y: 5 })}>Evaluate Formula</button>
            <p>Formula Result: {formulaResult}</p>
        </div>
    );
}
export default App;
```

**main.py**
```python
'''
Main entry point for the Django application.
'''
import os
import sys
from django.core.wsgi import get_wsgi_application

os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'myproject.settings')
application = get_wsgi_application()
```

**views.py**
```python
'''
Django views for handling document uploads and formula operations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt
from .models import Document, Formula
from .nlp_utils import summarize_text
from .formula_utils import evaluate_formula
import json

@csrf_exempt
def upload_documents(request):
    '''
    Handle document uploads and save them to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        files = request.FILES.getlist('documents')
        for file in files:
            content = file.read().decode('utf-8')
            Document.objects.create(title=file.name, content=content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Documents uploaded successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})

@csrf_exempt
def generate_summary(request, document_id):
    '''
    Generate a summary for a specific document.
    '''
    try:
        document = Document.objects.get(id=document_id)
        summary = summarize_text(document.content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'summary': summary})
    except Document.DoesNotExist:
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Document not found.'})

@csrf_exempt
def save_formula(request):
    '''
    Save a new formula to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        name = data.get('name')
        expression = data.get('expression')
        Formula.objects.create(name=name, expression=expression)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Formula saved successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})

@csrf_exempt
def evaluate_formula_view(request):
    '''
    Evaluate a formula using provided variables.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        formula_id = data.get('formula_id')
        variables = data.get('variables', {})
        try:
            formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id)
            result = evaluate_formula(formula.expression, variables)
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'result': result})
        except Formula.DoesNotExist:
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Formula not found.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
```

**models.py**
```python
'''
Django models for storing documents and formulas.
'''
from django.db import models

class Document(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()

class Formula(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    expression = models.TextField()
```

**nlp_utils.py**
```python
'''
NLP utilities for text summarization.
'''
import spacy

nlp = spacy.load("en_core_web_sm")

def summarize_text(text):
    '''
    Simple summarization logic.
    '''
    doc = nlp(text)
    summary = ' '.join([sent.text for sent in doc.sents][:3])  # Example: first 3 sentences
    return summary
```

**formula_utils.py**
```python
'''
Utilities for formula evaluation.
'''
def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
    '''
    Evaluate the formula using the provided variables.
    '''
    try:
        result = eval(expression, {}, variables)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        return str(e)
```

**gui.py**
```python
'''
PyQt5 GUI implementation for the application.
'''
from PyQt5.QtWidgets import QMainWindow, QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QPushButton, QLabel, QFileDialog

class MainWindow(QMainWindow):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setWindowTitle("Document Summarizer and Formula Builder")
        self.setGeometry(100, 100, 800, 600)
        self.central_widget = QWidget()
        self.setCentralWidget(self.central_widget)
        self.layout = QVBoxLayout()
        self.central_widget.setLayout(self.layout)
        self.upload_button = QPushButton("Upload Documents")
        self.upload_button.clicked.connect(self.upload_documents)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.upload_button)
        self.summary_label = QLabel("Summary will appear here.")
        self.layout.addWidget(self.summary_label)
        self.formula_button = QPushButton("Evaluate Formula")
        self.formula_button.clicked.connect(self.evaluate_formula)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.formula_button)

    def upload_documents(self):
        '''
        Logic to handle document upload.
        '''
        file_dialog = QFileDialog()
        file_dialog.setFileMode(QFileDialog.ExistingFiles)
        file_dialog.setNameFilter("Text files (*.txt)")
        if file_dialog.exec_():
            file_names = file_dialog.selectedFiles()
            # Process files
            self.summary_label.setText("Documents uploaded.")

    def evaluate_formula(self):
        '''
        Logic to evaluate a formula.
        '''
        self.summary_label.setText("Formula evaluated.")
```

**app.js**
```javascript
'''
React component for the main application interface.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

function App() {
    const [documents, setDocuments] = useState([]);
    const [summary, setSummary] = useState('');
    const [formulaResult, setFormulaResult] = useState('');

    const uploadDocuments = async (event) => {
        const files = event.target.files;
        const formData = new FormData();
        for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
            formData.append('documents', files[i]);
        }
        const response = await axios.post('/upload_documents', formData);
        console.log(response.data.message);
    };

    const generateSummary = async (documentId) => {
        const response = await axios.get(`/generate_summary/${documentId}`);
        setSummary(response.data.summary);
    };

    const evaluateFormula = async (formulaId, variables) => {
        const response = await axios.post('/evaluate_formula_view', { formula_id: formulaId, variables });
        setFormulaResult(response.data.result);
    };

    return (
        <div>
            <h1>Document Summarizer and Formula Builder</h1>
            <input type="file" multiple onChange={uploadDocuments} />
            <button onClick={() => generateSummary(1)}>Generate Summary</button>
            <p>Summary: {summary}</p>
            <button onClick={() => evaluateFormula(1, { x: 10, y: 5 })}>Evaluate Formula</button>
            <p>Formula Result: {formulaResult}</p>
        </div>
    );
}

export default App;
```

```python
from .models import Document, Formula

from .formula_utils import evaluate_formula

@csrf_exempt
def upload_documents(request):
    '''
    Handle document uploads and save them to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        files = request.FILES.getlist('documents')
        for file in files:
            content = file.read().decode('utf-8')
            Document.objects.create(title=file.name, content=content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Documents uploaded successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})

@csrf_exempt
def generate_summary(request, document_id):
    '''
    Generate a summary for a specific document.
    '''
    try:
        document = Document.objects.get(id=document_id)
        summary = summarize_text(document.content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'summary': summary})
    except Document.DoesNotExist:
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Document not found.'})

@csrf_exempt
def save_formula(request):
    '''
    Save a new formula to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        name = data.get('name')
        expression = data.get('expression')
        Formula.objects.create(name=name, expression=expression)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Formula saved successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})

@csrf_exempt
def evaluate_formula_view(request):
    '''
    Evaluate a formula using provided variables.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        formula_id = data.get('formula_id')
        variables = data.get('variables', {})
        try:
            formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id)
            result = evaluate_formula(formula.expression, variables)
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'result': result})

            return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Formula not found.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
```

"main.py
```python
'''
Main entry point for the Django application.
'''
import os
import sys
from django.core.wsgi import get_wsgi_application
os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'myproject.settings')
application = get_wsgi_application()
```

views.py
```python
'''
Django views for handling document uploads and formula operations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt
from .models import Document, Formula
from .nlp_utils import summarize_text
from .formula_utils import evaluate_formula
import json
@csrf_exempt
def upload_documents(request):
    '''
    Handle document uploads and save them to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        files = request.FILES.getlist('documents')
        for file in files:
            content = file.read().decode('utf-8')
            Document.objects.create(title=file.name, content=content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Documents uploaded successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def generate_summary(request, document_id):
    '''
    Generate a summary for a specific document.
    '''
    try:
        document = Document.objects.get(id=document_id)
        summary = summarize_text(document.content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'summary': summary})
    except Document.DoesNotExist:
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Document not found.'})
@csrf_exempt
def save_formula(request):
    '''
    Save a new formula to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        name = data.get('name')
        expression = data.get('expression')
        Formula.objects.create(name=name, expression=expression)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Formula saved successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def evaluate_formula_view(request):
    '''
    Evaluate a formula using provided variables.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        formula_id = data.get('formula_id')
        variables = data.get('variables', {})
        try:
            formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id)
            result = evaluate_formula(formula.expression, variables)
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'result': result})
        except Formula.DoesNotExist:
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Formula not found.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Django models for storing documents and formulas.
'''
from django.db import models
class Document(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()
class Formula(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    expression = models.TextField()
```

nlp_utils.py
```python
'''
NLP utilities for text summarization.
'''
import spacy
nlp = spacy.load("en_core_web_sm")
def summarize_text(text):
    '''
    Simple summarization logic.
    '''
    doc = nlp(text)
    summary = ' '.join([sent.text for sent in doc.sents][:3])  # Example: first 3 sentences
    return summary
```

formula_utils.py
```python
'''
Utilities for formula evaluation.
'''
def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
    '''
    Evaluate the formula using the provided variables.
    '''
    try:
        result = eval(expression, {}, variables)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        return str(e)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
PyQt5 GUI implementation for the application.
'''
from PyQt5.QtWidgets import QMainWindow, QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QPushButton, QLabel, QFileDialog
class MainWindow(QMainWindow):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setWindowTitle("Document Summarizer and Formula Builder")
        self.setGeometry(100, 100, 800, 600)
        self.central_widget = QWidget()
        self.setCentralWidget(self.central_widget)
        self.layout = QVBoxLayout()
        self.central_widget.setLayout(self.layout)
        self.upload_button = QPushButton("Upload Documents")
        self.upload_button.clicked.connect(self.upload_documents)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.upload_button)
        self.summary_label = QLabel("Summary will appear here.")
        self.layout.addWidget(self.summary_label)
        self.formula_button = QPushButton("Evaluate Formula")
        self.formula_button.clicked.connect(self.evaluate_formula)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.formula_button)
    def upload_documents(self):
        '''
        Logic to handle document upload.
        '''
        file_dialog = QFileDialog()
        file_dialog.setFileMode(QFileDialog.ExistingFiles)
        file_dialog.setNameFilter("Text files (*.txt)")
        if file_dialog.exec_():
            file_names = file_dialog.selectedFiles()
            # Process files
            self.summary_label.setText("Documents uploaded.")
    def evaluate_formula(self):
        '''
        Logic to evaluate a formula.
        '''
        self.summary_label.setText("Formula evaluated.")
```

app.js
```js
'''
React component for the main application interface.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function App() {
    const [documents, setDocuments] = useState([]);
    const [summary, setSummary] = useState('');
    const [formulaResult, setFormulaResult] = useState('');
    const uploadDocuments = async (event) => {
        const files = event.target.files;
        const formData = new FormData();
        for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
            formData.append('documents', files[i]);
        }
        const response = await axios.post('/upload_documents', formData);
        console.log(response.data.message);
    };
    const generateSummary = async (documentId) => {
        const response = await axios.get(`/generate_summary/${documentId}`);
        setSummary(response.data.summary);
    };
    const evaluateFormula = async (formulaId, variables) => {
        const response = await axios.post('/evaluate_formula_view', { formula_id: formulaId, variables });
        setFormulaResult(response.data.result);
    };
    return (
        <div>
            <h1>Document Summarizer and Formula Builder</h1>
            <input type="file" multiple onChange={uploadDocuments} />
            <button onClick={() => generateSummary(1)}>Generate Summary</button>
            <p>Summary: {summary}</p>
            <button onClick={() => evaluateFormula(1, { x: 10, y: 5 })}>Evaluate Formula</button>
            <p>Formula Result: {formulaResult}</p>
        </div>
    );
}
export default App;
```

The highest priority issue in the provided code is the use of the `eval` function in `formula_utils.py` for evaluating formulas. This poses a significant security risk as it can execute arbitrary code. Instead, consider using a safer alternative like the `asteval` library, which provides a safer environment for evaluating mathematical expressions.

**Suggestion for Revision:**

1. Install the `asteval` library:
   ```bash
   pip install asteval
   ```

2. Modify `formula_utils.py` to use `asteval`:
   ```python
   '''
   Utilities for formula evaluation.
   '''
   from asteval import Interpreter

   def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
       '''
       Evaluate the formula using the provided variables.
       '''
       try:
           aeval = Interpreter()
           for key, value in variables.items():
               aeval.symtable[key] = value
           result = aeval(expression)
           return result
       except Exception as e:
           return str(e)
   ```

This change will mitigate the security risks associated with using `eval` while still allowing for flexible formula evaluation.

```python
'''
Main entry point for the Django application.
'''
import os
import sys
from django.core.wsgi import get_wsgi_application
os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'myproject.settings')
application = get_wsgi_application()
```

views.py
```python
'''
Django views for handling document uploads and formula operations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt
from .models import Document, Formula
from .nlp_utils import summarize_text
from .formula_utils import evaluate_formula
import json
@csrf_exempt
def upload_documents(request):
    '''
    Handle document uploads and save them to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        files = request.FILES.getlist('documents')
        for file in files:
            content = file.read().decode('utf-8')
            Document.objects.create(title=file.name, content=content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Documents uploaded successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def generate_summary(request, document_id):
    '''
    Generate a summary for a specific document.
    '''
    try:
        document = Document.objects.get(id=document_id)
        summary = summarize_text(document.content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'summary': summary})
    except Document.DoesNotExist:
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Document not found.'})
@csrf_exempt
def save_formula(request):
    '''
    Save a new formula to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        name = data.get('name')
        expression = data.get('expression')
        Formula.objects.create(name=name, expression=expression)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Formula saved successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def evaluate_formula_view(request):
    '''
    Evaluate a formula using provided variables.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        formula_id = data.get('formula_id')
        variables = data.get('variables', {})
        try:
            formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id)
            result = evaluate_formula(formula.expression, variables)
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'result': result})
        except Formula.DoesNotExist:
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Formula not found.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Django models for storing documents and formulas.
'''
from django.db import models
class Document(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()
class Formula(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    expression = models.TextField()
```

nlp_utils.py
```python
'''
NLP utilities for text summarization.
'''
import spacy
nlp = spacy.load("en_core_web_sm")
def summarize_text(text):
    '''
    Simple summarization logic.
    '''
    doc = nlp(text)
    summary = ' '.join([sent.text for sent in doc.sents][:3])  # Example: first 3 sentences
    return summary
```

formula_utils.py
```python
'''
Utilities for formula evaluation.
'''
def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
    '''
    Evaluate the formula using the provided variables.
    '''
    try:
        result = eval(expression, {}, variables)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        return str(e)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
PyQt5 GUI implementation for the application.
'''
from PyQt5.QtWidgets import QMainWindow, QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QPushButton, QLabel, QFileDialog
class MainWindow(QMainWindow):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setWindowTitle("Document Summarizer and Formula Builder")
        self.setGeometry(100, 100, 800, 600)
        self.central_widget = QWidget()
        self.setCentralWidget(self.central_widget)
        self.layout = QVBoxLayout()
        self.central_widget.setLayout(self.layout)
        self.upload_button = QPushButton("Upload Documents")
        self.upload_button.clicked.connect(self.upload_documents)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.upload_button)
        self.summary_label = QLabel("Summary will appear here.")
        self.layout.addWidget(self.summary_label)
        self.formula_button = QPushButton("Evaluate Formula")
        self.formula_button.clicked.connect(self.evaluate_formula)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.formula_button)
    def upload_documents(self):
        '''
        Logic to handle document upload.
        '''
        file_dialog = QFileDialog()
        file_dialog.setFileMode(QFileDialog.ExistingFiles)
        file_dialog.setNameFilter("Text files (*.txt)")
        if file_dialog.exec_():
            file_names = file_dialog.selectedFiles()
            # Process files
            self.summary_label.setText("Documents uploaded.")
    def evaluate_formula(self):
        '''
        Logic to evaluate a formula.
        '''
        self.summary_label.setText("Formula evaluated.")
```

app.js
```js
'''
React component for the main application interface.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function App() {
    const [documents, setDocuments] = useState([]);
    const [summary, setSummary] = useState('');
    const [formulaResult, setFormulaResult] = useState('');
    const uploadDocuments = async (event) => {
        const files = event.target.files;
        const formData = new FormData();
        for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
            formData.append('documents', files[i]);
        }
        const response = await axios.post('/upload_documents', formData);
        console.log(response.data.message);
    };
    const generateSummary = async (documentId) => {
        const response = await axios.get(`/generate_summary/${documentId}`);
        setSummary(response.data.summary);
    };
    const evaluateFormula = async (formulaId, variables) => {
        const response = await axios.post('/evaluate_formula_view', { formula_id: formulaId, variables });
        setFormulaResult(response.data.result);
    };
    return (
        <div>
            <h1>Document Summarizer and Formula Builder</h1>
            <input type="file" multiple onChange={uploadDocuments} />
            <button onClick={() => generateSummary(1)}>Generate Summary</button>
            <p>Summary: {summary}</p>
            <button onClick={() => evaluateFormula(1, { x: 10, y: 5 })}>Evaluate Formula</button>
            <p>Formula Result: {formulaResult}</p>
        </div>
    );
}
export default App;
```

"The highest priority issue in the provided code is the use of the `eval` function in `formula_utils.py` for evaluating formulas. This poses a significant security risk as it can execute arbitrary code. Instead, consider using a safer alternative like the `asteval` library, which provides a safer environment for evaluating mathematical expressions.

**Suggestion for Revision:**

1. Install the `asteval` library:
   ```bash
   pip install asteval
   ```

2. Modify `formula_utils.py` to use `asteval`:
   ```python
   '''
   Utilities for formula evaluation.
   '''
   from asteval import Interpreter

   def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
       '''
       Evaluate the formula using the provided variables.
       '''
       try:
           aeval = Interpreter()
           for key, value in variables.items():
               aeval.symtable[key] = value
           result = aeval(expression)
           return result
       except Exception as e:
           return str(e)
   ```

This change will mitigate the security risks associated with using `eval` while still allowing for flexible formula evaluation."

```python
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt
from .models import Document, Formula
from .nlp_utils import summarize_text
from .formula_utils import evaluate_formula
import json

@csrf_exempt
def upload_documents(request):
    '''
    Handle document uploads and save them to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        files = request.FILES.getlist('documents')
        for file in files:
            content = file.read().decode('utf-8')
            Document.objects.create(title=file.name, content=content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Documents uploaded successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})

@csrf_exempt
def generate_summary(request, document_id):
    '''
    Generate a summary for a specific document.
    '''
    try:
        document = Document.objects.get(id=document_id)
        summary = summarize_text(document.content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'summary': summary})
    except Document.DoesNotExist:
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Document not found.'})

@csrf_exempt
def save_formula(request):
    '''
    Save a new formula to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        name = data.get('name')
        expression = data.get('expression')
        Formula.objects.create(name=name, expression=expression)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Formula saved successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})

@csrf_exempt
def evaluate_formula_view(request):
    '''
    Evaluate a formula using provided variables.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        formula_id = data.get('formula_id')
        variables = data.get('variables', {})
        try:
            formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id)
            result = evaluate_formula(formula.expression, variables)
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'result': result})
        except Formula.DoesNotExist:
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Formula not found.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Django models for storing documents and formulas.
'''
from django.db import models

class Document(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()

class Formula(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    expression = models.TextField()
```

nlp_utils.py
```python
'''
NLP utilities for text summarization.
'''
import spacy

nlp = spacy.load("en_core_web_sm")

def summarize_text(text):
    '''
    Simple summarization logic.
    '''
    doc = nlp(text)
    summary = ' '.join([sent.text for sent in doc.sents][:3])  # Example: first 3 sentences
    return summary
```

formula_utils.py
```python
'''
Utilities for formula evaluation.
'''
from asteval import Interpreter

def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
    '''
    Evaluate the formula using the provided variables.
    '''
    try:
        aeval = Interpreter()
        for key, value in variables.items():
            aeval.symtable[key] = value
        result = aeval(expression)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        return str(e)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
PyQt5 GUI implementation for the application.
'''
from PyQt5.QtWidgets import QMainWindow, QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QPushButton, QLabel, QFileDialog

class MainWindow(QMainWindow):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setWindowTitle("Document Summarizer and Formula Builder")
        self.setGeometry(100, 100, 800, 600)
        self.central_widget = QWidget()
        self.setCentralWidget(self.central_widget)
        self.layout = QVBoxLayout()
        self.central_widget.setLayout(self.layout)
        self.upload_button = QPushButton("Upload Documents")
        self.upload_button.clicked.connect(self.upload_documents)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.upload_button)
        self.summary_label = QLabel("Summary will appear here.")
        self.layout.addWidget(self.summary_label)
        self.formula_button = QPushButton("Evaluate Formula")
        self.formula_button.clicked.connect(self.evaluate_formula)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.formula_button)

    def upload_documents(self):
        '''
        Logic to handle document upload.
        '''
        file_dialog = QFileDialog()
        file_dialog.setFileMode(QFileDialog.ExistingFiles)
        file_dialog.setNameFilter("Text files (*.txt)")
        if file_dialog.exec_():
            file_names = file_dialog.selectedFiles()
            # Process files
            self.summary_label.setText("Documents uploaded.")

    def evaluate_formula(self):
        '''
        Logic to evaluate a formula.
        '''
        self.summary_label.setText("Formula evaluated.")
```

app.js
```javascript
'''
React component for the main application interface.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

function App() {
    const [documents, setDocuments] = useState([]);
    const [summary, setSummary] = useState('');
    const [formulaResult, setFormulaResult] = useState('');

    const uploadDocuments = async (event) => {
        const files = event.target.files;
        const formData = new FormData();
        for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
            formData.append('documents', files[i]);
        }
        const response = await axios.post('/upload_documents', formData);
        console.log(response.data.message);
    };

    const generateSummary = async (documentId) => {
        const response = await axios.get(`/generate_summary/${documentId}`);
        setSummary(response.data.summary);
    };

    const evaluateFormula = async (formulaId, variables) => {
        const response = await axios.post('/evaluate_formula_view', { formula_id: formulaId, variables });
        setFormulaResult(response.data.result);
    };

    return (
        <div>
            <h1>Document Summarizer and Formula Builder</h1>
            <input type="file" multiple onChange={uploadDocuments} />
            <button onClick={() => generateSummary(1)}>Generate Summary</button>
            <p>Summary: {summary}</p>
            <button onClick={() => evaluateFormula(1, { x: 10, y: 5 })}>Evaluate Formula</button>
            <p>Formula Result: {formulaResult}</p>
        </div>
    );
}

export default App;
```

```python
from django.shortcuts import render
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt
from .models import Document, Formula
from .nlp_utils import summarize_text
from .formula_utils import evaluate_formula

@csrf_exempt
def upload_documents(request):

    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})

@csrf_exempt
def generate_summary(request, document_id):

        expression = data.get('expression')

        try:
```

formula_utils.py
```python
'''
Utilities for formula evaluation.
'''
from asteval import Interpreter

def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
    '''
    Evaluate the formula using the provided variables.
    '''
    try:
        aeval = Interpreter()
        for key, value in variables.items():
            aeval.symtable[key] = value
        result = aeval(expression)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        return str(e)
```

views.py
```python
'''
Django views for handling document uploads and formula operations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt
from .models import Document, Formula
from .nlp_utils import summarize_text
from .formula_utils import evaluate_formula
import json
@csrf_exempt
def upload_documents(request):
    '''
    Handle document uploads and save them to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        files = request.FILES.getlist('documents')
        for file in files:
            content = file.read().decode('utf-8')
            Document.objects.create(title=file.name, content=content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Documents uploaded successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def generate_summary(request, document_id):
    '''
    Generate a summary for a specific document.
    '''
    try:
        document = Document.objects.get(id=document_id)
        summary = summarize_text(document.content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'summary': summary})
    except Document.DoesNotExist:
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Document not found.'})
@csrf_exempt
def save_formula(request):
    '''
    Save a new formula to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        name = data.get('name')
        expression = data.get('expression')
        Formula.objects.create(name=name, expression=expression)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Formula saved successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def evaluate_formula_view(request):
    '''
    Evaluate a formula using provided variables.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        formula_id = data.get('formula_id')
        variables = data.get('variables', {})
        try:
            formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id)
            result = evaluate_formula(formula.expression, variables)
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'result': result})
        except Formula.DoesNotExist:
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Formula not found.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Django models for storing documents and formulas.
'''
from django.db import models
class Document(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()
class Formula(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    expression = models.TextField()
```

nlp_utils.py
```python
'''
NLP utilities for text summarization.
'''
import spacy
nlp = spacy.load("en_core_web_sm")
def summarize_text(text):
    '''
    Simple summarization logic.
    '''
    doc = nlp(text)
    summary = ' '.join([sent.text for sent in doc.sents][:3])  # Example: first 3 sentences
    return summary
```

formula_utils.py
```python
'''
Utilities for formula evaluation.
'''
from asteval import Interpreter
def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
    '''
    Evaluate the formula using the provided variables.
    '''
    try:
        aeval = Interpreter()
        for key, value in variables.items():
            aeval.symtable[key] = value
        result = aeval(expression)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        return str(e)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
PyQt5 GUI implementation for the application.
'''
from PyQt5.QtWidgets import QMainWindow, QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QPushButton, QLabel, QFileDialog
class MainWindow(QMainWindow):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setWindowTitle("Document Summarizer and Formula Builder")
        self.setGeometry(100, 100, 800, 600)
        self.central_widget = QWidget()
        self.setCentralWidget(self.central_widget)
        self.layout = QVBoxLayout()
        self.central_widget.setLayout(self.layout)
        self.upload_button = QPushButton("Upload Documents")
        self.upload_button.clicked.connect(self.upload_documents)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.upload_button)
        self.summary_label = QLabel("Summary will appear here.")
        self.layout.addWidget(self.summary_label)
        self.formula_button = QPushButton("Evaluate Formula")
        self.formula_button.clicked.connect(self.evaluate_formula)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.formula_button)
    def upload_documents(self):
        '''
        Logic to handle document upload.
        '''
        file_dialog = QFileDialog()
        file_dialog.setFileMode(QFileDialog.ExistingFiles)
        file_dialog.setNameFilter("Text files (*.txt)")
        if file_dialog.exec_():
            file_names = file_dialog.selectedFiles()
            # Process files
            self.summary_label.setText("Documents uploaded.")
    def evaluate_formula(self):
        '''
        Logic to evaluate a formula.
        '''
        self.summary_label.setText("Formula evaluated.")
```

app.js
```js
'''
React component for the main application interface.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function App() {
    const [documents, setDocuments] = useState([]);
    const [summary, setSummary] = useState('');
    const [formulaResult, setFormulaResult] = useState('');
    const uploadDocuments = async (event) => {
        const files = event.target.files;
        const formData = new FormData();
        for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
            formData.append('documents', files[i]);
        }
        const response = await axios.post('/upload_documents', formData);
        console.log(response.data.message);
    };
    const generateSummary = async (documentId) => {
        const response = await axios.get(`/generate_summary/${documentId}`);
        setSummary(response.data.summary);
    };
    const evaluateFormula = async (formulaId, variables) => {
        const response = await axios.post('/evaluate_formula_view', { formula_id: formulaId, variables });
        setFormulaResult(response.data.result);
    };
    return (
        <div>
            <h1>Document Summarizer and Formula Builder</h1>
            <input type="file" multiple onChange={uploadDocuments} />
            <button onClick={() => generateSummary(1)}>Generate Summary</button>
            <p>Summary: {summary}</p>
            <button onClick={() => evaluateFormula(1, { x: 10, y: 5 })}>Evaluate Formula</button>
            <p>Formula Result: {formulaResult}</p>
        </div>
    );
}
export default App;
```
