'''
Main entry point for the Django application.
'''
import os
import sys
from django.core.wsgi import get_wsgi_application
os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'myproject.settings')
application = get_wsgi_application()
```

views.py
```python
'''
Django views for handling document uploads and formula operations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt
from .models import Document, Formula
from .nlp_utils import summarize_text
from .formula_utils import evaluate_formula
import json
@csrf_exempt
def upload_documents(request):
    '''
    Handle document uploads and save them to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        files = request.FILES.getlist('documents')
        for file in files:
            content = file.read().decode('utf-8')
            Document.objects.create(title=file.name, content=content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Documents uploaded successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def generate_summary(request, document_id):
    '''
    Generate a summary for a specific document.
    '''
    try:
        document = Document.objects.get(id=document_id)
        summary = summarize_text(document.content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'summary': summary})
    except Document.DoesNotExist:
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Document not found.'})
@csrf_exempt
def save_formula(request):
    '''
    Save a new formula to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        name = data.get('name')
        expression = data.get('expression')
        Formula.objects.create(name=name, expression=expression)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Formula saved successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def evaluate_formula_view(request):
    '''
    Evaluate a formula using provided variables.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        formula_id = data.get('formula_id')
        variables = data.get('variables', {})
        try:
            formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id)
            result = evaluate_formula(formula.expression, variables)
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'result': result})
        except Formula.DoesNotExist:
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Formula not found.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Django models for storing documents and formulas.
'''
from django.db import models
class Document(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()
class Formula(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    expression = models.TextField()
```

nlp_utils.py
```python
'''
NLP utilities for text summarization.
'''
import spacy
nlp = spacy.load("en_core_web_sm")
def summarize_text(text):
    '''
    Simple summarization logic.
    '''
    doc = nlp(text)
    summary = ' '.join([sent.text for sent in doc.sents][:3])  # Example: first 3 sentences
    return summary
```

formula_utils.py
```python
'''
Utilities for formula evaluation.
'''
from asteval import Interpreter
def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
    '''
    Evaluate the formula using the provided variables.
    '''
    try:
        aeval = Interpreter()
        for key, value in variables.items():
            aeval.symtable[key] = value
        result = aeval(expression)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        return str(e)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
PyQt5 GUI implementation for the application.
'''
from PyQt5.QtWidgets import QMainWindow, QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QPushButton, QLabel, QFileDialog
class MainWindow(QMainWindow):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setWindowTitle("Document Summarizer and Formula Builder")
        self.setGeometry(100, 100, 800, 600)
        self.central_widget = QWidget()
        self.setCentralWidget(self.central_widget)
        self.layout = QVBoxLayout()
        self.central_widget.setLayout(self.layout)
        self.upload_button = QPushButton("Upload Documents")
        self.upload_button.clicked.connect(self.upload_documents)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.upload_button)
        self.summary_label = QLabel("Summary will appear here.")
        self.layout.addWidget(self.summary_label)
        self.formula_button = QPushButton("Evaluate Formula")
        self.formula_button.clicked.connect(self.evaluate_formula)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.formula_button)
    def upload_documents(self):
        '''
        Logic to handle document upload.
        '''
        file_dialog = QFileDialog()
        file_dialog.setFileMode(QFileDialog.ExistingFiles)
        file_dialog.setNameFilter("Text files (*.txt)")
        if file_dialog.exec_():
            file_names = file_dialog.selectedFiles()
            # Process files
            self.summary_label.setText("Documents uploaded.")
    def evaluate_formula(self):
        '''
        Logic to evaluate a formula.
        '''
        self.summary_label.setText("Formula evaluated.")
```

app.js
```js
'''
React component for the main application interface.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function App() {
    const [documents, setDocuments] = useState([]);
    const [summary, setSummary] = useState('');
    const [formulaResult, setFormulaResult] = useState('');
    const uploadDocuments = async (event) => {
        const files = event.target.files;
        const formData = new FormData();
        for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
            formData.append('documents', files[i]);
        }
        const response = await axios.post('/upload_documents', formData);
        console.log(response.data.message);
    };
    const generateSummary = async (documentId) => {
        const response = await axios.get(`/generate_summary/${documentId}`);
        setSummary(response.data.summary);
    };
    const evaluateFormula = async (formulaId, variables) => {
        const response = await axios.post('/evaluate_formula_view', { formula_id: formulaId, variables });
        setFormulaResult(response.data.result);
    };
    return (
        <div>
            <h1>Document Summarizer and Formula Builder</h1>
            <input type="file" multiple onChange={uploadDocuments} />
            <button onClick={() => generateSummary(1)}>Generate Summary</button>
            <p>Summary: {summary}</p>
            <button onClick={() => evaluateFormula(1, { x: 10, y: 5 })}>Evaluate Formula</button>
            <p>Formula Result: {formulaResult}</p>
        </div>
    );
}
export default App;
```

.py
```python
'''
Main entry point for the Django application.
'''
import os
import sys
from django.core.wsgi import get_wsgi_application
# Correct the project settings module name
os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'your_project_name.settings')
application = get_wsgi_application()

'''
Main entry point for the Django application.
'''
import os
import sys
from django.core.wsgi import get_wsgi_application
os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'myproject.settings')
application = get_wsgi_application()
```

views.py
```python
'''
Django views for handling document uploads and formula operations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt
from .models import Document, Formula
from .nlp_utils import summarize_text
from .formula_utils import evaluate_formula
import json
@csrf_exempt
def upload_documents(request):
    '''
    Handle document uploads and save them to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        files = request.FILES.getlist('documents')
        for file in files:
            content = file.read().decode('utf-8')
            Document.objects.create(title=file.name, content=content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Documents uploaded successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def generate_summary(request, document_id):
    '''
    Generate a summary for a specific document.
    '''
    try:
        document = Document.objects.get(id=document_id)
        summary = summarize_text(document.content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'summary': summary})
    except Document.DoesNotExist:
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Document not found.'})
@csrf_exempt
def save_formula(request):
    '''
    Save a new formula to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        name = data.get('name')
        expression = data.get('expression')
        Formula.objects.create(name=name, expression=expression)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Formula saved successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def evaluate_formula_view(request):
    '''
    Evaluate a formula using provided variables.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        formula_id = data.get('formula_id')
        variables = data.get('variables', {})
        try:
            formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id)
            result = evaluate_formula(formula.expression, variables)
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'result': result})
        except Formula.DoesNotExist:
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Formula not found.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Django models for storing documents and formulas.
'''
from django.db import models
class Document(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()
class Formula(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    expression = models.TextField()
```

nlp_utils.py
```python
'''
NLP utilities for text summarization.
'''
import spacy
nlp = spacy.load("en_core_web_sm")
def summarize_text(text):
    '''
    Simple summarization logic.
    '''
    doc = nlp(text)
    summary = ' '.join([sent.text for sent in doc.sents][:3])  # Example: first 3 sentences
    return summary
```

formula_utils.py
```python
'''
Utilities for formula evaluation.
'''
from asteval import Interpreter
def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
    '''
    Evaluate the formula using the provided variables.
    '''
    try:
        aeval = Interpreter()
        for key, value in variables.items():
            aeval.symtable[key] = value
        result = aeval(expression)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        return str(e)
```

'''
PyQt5 GUI implementation for the application.

from PyQt5.QtWidgets import QMainWindow, QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QPushButton, QLabel, QFileDialog
class MainWindow(QMainWindow):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setWindowTitle("Document Summarizer and Formula Builder")
        self.setGeometry(100, 100, 800, 600)
        self.central_widget = QWidget()
        self.setCentralWidget(self.central_widget)
        self.layout = QVBoxLayout()
        self.central_widget.setLayout(self.layout)
        self.upload_button = QPushButton("Upload Documents")
        self.upload_button.clicked.connect(self.upload_documents)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.upload_button)
        self.summary_label = QLabel("Summary will appear here.")
        self.layout.addWidget(self.summary_label)
        self.formula_button = QPushButton("Evaluate Formula")
        self.formula_button.clicked.connect(self.evaluate_formula)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.formula_button)
    def upload_documents(self):
        '''
        Logic to handle document upload.
        '''
        file_dialog = QFileDialog()
        file_dialog.setFileMode(QFileDialog.ExistingFiles)
        file_dialog.setNameFilter("Text files (*.txt)")
        if file_dialog.exec_():
            file_names = file_dialog.selectedFiles()
            # Process files
            self.summary_label.setText("Documents uploaded.")
    def evaluate_formula(self):
        '''
        Logic to evaluate a formula.
        '''
        self.summary_label.setText("Formula evaluated.")

app.js
```js
'''
React component for the main application interface.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function App() {
    const [documents, setDocuments] = useState([]);
    const [summary, setSummary] = useState('');
    const [formulaResult, setFormulaResult] = useState('');
    const uploadDocuments = async (event) => {
        const files = event.target.files;
        const formData = new FormData();
        for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
            formData.append('documents', files[i]);
        }
        const response = await axios.post('/upload_documents', formData);
        console.log(response.data.message);
    };
    const generateSummary = async (documentId) => {
        const response = await axios.get(`/generate_summary/${documentId}`);
        setSummary(response.data.summary);
    };
    const evaluateFormula = async (formulaId, variables) => {
        const response = await axios.post('/evaluate_formula_view', { formula_id: formulaId, variables });
        setFormulaResult(response.data.result);
    };
    return (
        <div>
            <h1>Document Summarizer and Formula Builder</h1>
            <input type="file" multiple onChange={uploadDocuments} />
            <button onClick={() => generateSummary(1)}>Generate Summary</button>
            <p>Summary: {summary}</p>
            <button onClick={() => evaluateFormula(1, { x: 10, y: 5 })}>Evaluate Formula</button>
            <p>Formula Result: {formulaResult}</p>
        </div>
    );
}
export default App;
```

```python
'''
Main entry point for the Django application.
'''
import os
import sys
from django.core.wsgi import get_wsgi_application
os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'myproject.settings')
application = get_wsgi_application()

views.py
```python
'''
Django views for handling document uploads and formula operations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt
from .models import Document, Formula
from .nlp_utils import summarize_text
from .formula_utils import evaluate_formula
import json
@csrf_exempt
def upload_documents(request):
    '''
    Handle document uploads and save them to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        files = request.FILES.getlist('documents')
        for file in files:
            content = file.read().decode('utf-8')
            Document.objects.create(title=file.name, content=content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Documents uploaded successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def generate_summary(request, document_id):
    '''
    Generate a summary for a specific document.
    '''
    try:
        document = Document.objects.get(id=document_id)
        summary = summarize_text(document.content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'summary': summary})
    except Document.DoesNotExist:
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Document not found.'})
@csrf_exempt
def save_formula(request):
    '''
    Save a new formula to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        name = data.get('name')
        expression = data.get('expression')
        Formula.objects.create(name=name, expression=expression)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Formula saved successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def evaluate_formula_view(request):
    '''
    Evaluate a formula using provided variables.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        formula_id = data.get('formula_id')
        variables = data.get('variables', {})
        try:
            formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id)
            result = evaluate_formula(formula.expression, variables)
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'result': result})
        except Formula.DoesNotExist:
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Formula not found.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Django models for storing documents and formulas.
'''
from django.db import models
class Document(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()
class Formula(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    expression = models.TextField()
```

nlp_utils.py
```python
'''
NLP utilities for text summarization.
'''
import spacy
nlp = spacy.load("en_core_web_sm")
def summarize_text(text):
    '''
    Simple summarization logic.
    '''
    doc = nlp(text)
    summary = ' '.join([sent.text for sent in doc.sents][:3])  # Example: first 3 sentences
    return summary
```

formula_utils.py
```python
'''
Utilities for formula evaluation.
'''
from asteval import Interpreter
def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
    '''
    Evaluate the formula using the provided variables.
    '''
    try:
        aeval = Interpreter()
        for key, value in variables.items():
            aeval.symtable[key] = value
        result = aeval(expression)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        return str(e)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
PyQt5 GUI implementation for the application.
'''
from PyQt5.QtWidgets import QMainWindow, QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QPushButton, QLabel, QFileDialog
class MainWindow(QMainWindow):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setWindowTitle("Document Summarizer and Formula Builder")
        self.setGeometry(100, 100, 800, 600)
        self.central_widget = QWidget()
        self.setCentralWidget(self.central_widget)
        self.layout = QVBoxLayout()
        self.central_widget.setLayout(self.layout)
        self.upload_button = QPushButton("Upload Documents")
        self.upload_button.clicked.connect(self.upload_documents)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.upload_button)
        self.summary_label = QLabel("Summary will appear here.")
        self.layout.addWidget(self.summary_label)
        self.formula_button = QPushButton("Evaluate Formula")
        self.formula_button.clicked.connect(self.evaluate_formula)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.formula_button)
    def upload_documents(self):
        '''
        Logic to handle document upload.
        '''
        file_dialog = QFileDialog()
        file_dialog.setFileMode(QFileDialog.ExistingFiles)
        file_dialog.setNameFilter("Text files (*.txt)")
        if file_dialog.exec_():
            file_names = file_dialog.selectedFiles()
            # Process files
            self.summary_label.setText("Documents uploaded.")
    def evaluate_formula(self):
        '''
        Logic to evaluate a formula.
        '''
        self.summary_label.setText("Formula evaluated.")

app.js
```js
'''
React component for the main application interface.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function App() {
    const [documents, setDocuments] = useState([]);
    const [summary, setSummary] = useState('');
    const [formulaResult, setFormulaResult] = useState('');
    const uploadDocuments = async (event) => {
        const files = event.target.files;
        const formData = new FormData();
        for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
            formData.append('documents', files[i]);
        }
        const response = await axios.post('/upload_documents', formData);
        console.log(response.data.message);
    };
    const generateSummary = async (documentId) => {
        const response = await axios.get(`/generate_summary/${documentId}`);
        setSummary(response.data.summary);
    };
    const evaluateFormula = async (formulaId, variables) => {
        const response = await axios.post('/evaluate_formula_view', { formula_id: formulaId, variables });
        setFormulaResult(response.data.result);
    };
    return (
        <div>
            <h1>Document Summarizer and Formula Builder</h1>
            <input type="file" multiple onChange={uploadDocuments} />
            <button onClick={() => generateSummary(1)}>Generate Summary</button>
            <p>Summary: {summary}</p>
            <button onClick={() => evaluateFormula(1, { x: 10, y: 5 })}>Evaluate Formula</button>
            <p>Formula Result: {formulaResult}</p>
        </div>
    );
}
export default App;
```

"main.py
```python
'''
Main entry point for the Django application.
'''
import os
import sys
from django.core.wsgi import get_wsgi_application
os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'myproject.settings')
application = get_wsgi_application()
```
views.py
```python
'''
Django views for handling document uploads and formula operations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt
from .models import Document, Formula
from .nlp_utils import summarize_text
from .formula_utils import evaluate_formula
import json
@csrf_exempt
def upload_documents(request):
    '''
    Handle document uploads and save them to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        files = request.FILES.getlist('documents')
        for file in files:
            content = file.read().decode('utf-8')
            Document.objects.create(title=file.name, content=content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Documents uploaded successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def generate_summary(request, document_id):
    '''
    Generate a summary for a specific document.
    '''
    try:
        document = Document.objects.get(id=document_id)
        summary = summarize_text(document.content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'summary': summary})
    except Document.DoesNotExist:
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Document not found.'})
@csrf_exempt
def save_formula(request):
    '''
    Save a new formula to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        name = data.get('name')
        expression = data.get('expression')
        Formula.objects.create(name=name, expression=expression)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Formula saved successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def evaluate_formula_view(request):
    '''
    Evaluate a formula using provided variables.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        formula_id = data.get('formula_id')
        variables = data.get('variables', {})
        try:
            formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id)
            result = evaluate_formula(formula.expression, variables)
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'result': result})
        except Formula.DoesNotExist:
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Formula not found.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
```
models.py
```python
'''
Django models for storing documents and formulas.
'''
from django.db import models
class Document(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()
class Formula(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    expression = models.TextField()
```
nlp_utils.py
```python
'''
NLP utilities for text summarization.
'''
import spacy
nlp = spacy.load("en_core_web_sm")
def summarize_text(text):
    '''
    Simple summarization logic.
    '''
    doc = nlp(text)
    summary = ' '.join([sent.text for sent in doc.sents][:3])  # Example: first 3 sentences
    return summary
```
formula_utils.py
```python
'''
Utilities for formula evaluation.
'''
from asteval import Interpreter
def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
    '''
    Evaluate the formula using the provided variables.
    '''
    try:
        aeval = Interpreter()
        for key, value in variables.items():
            aeval.symtable[key] = value
        result = aeval(expression)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        return str(e)
```
gui.py
```python
'''
PyQt5 GUI implementation for the application.
'''
from PyQt5.QtWidgets import QMainWindow, QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QPushButton, QLabel, QFileDialog
class MainWindow(QMainWindow):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setWindowTitle("Document Summarizer and Formula Builder")
        self.setGeometry(100, 100, 800, 600)
        self.central_widget = QWidget()
        self.setCentralWidget(self.central_widget)
        self.layout = QVBoxLayout()
        self.central_widget.setLayout(self.layout)
        self.upload_button = QPushButton("Upload Documents")
        self.upload_button.clicked.connect(self.upload_documents)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.upload_button)
        self.summary_label = QLabel("Summary will appear here.")
        self.layout.addWidget(self.summary_label)
        self.formula_button = QPushButton("Evaluate Formula")
        self.formula_button.clicked.connect(self.evaluate_formula)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.formula_button)
    def upload_documents(self):
        '''
        Logic to handle document upload.
        '''
        file_dialog = QFileDialog()
        file_dialog.setFileMode(QFileDialog.ExistingFiles)
        file_dialog.setNameFilter("Text files (*.txt)")
        if file_dialog.exec_():
            file_names = file_dialog.selectedFiles()
            # Process files
            self.summary_label.setText("Documents uploaded.")
    def evaluate_formula(self):
        '''
        Logic to evaluate a formula.
        '''
        self.summary_label.setText("Formula evaluated.")

app.js
```js
'''
React component for the main application interface.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function App() {
    const [documents, setDocuments] = useState([]);
    const [summary, setSummary] = useState('');
    const [formulaResult, setFormulaResult] = useState('');
    const uploadDocuments = async (event) => {
        const files = event.target.files;
        const formData = new FormData();
        for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
            formData.append('documents', files[i]);
        }
        const response = await axios.post('/upload_documents', formData);
        console.log(response.data.message);
    };
    const generateSummary = async (documentId) => {
        const response = await axios.get(`/generate_summary/${documentId}`);
        setSummary(response.data.summary);
    };
    const evaluateFormula = async (formulaId, variables) => {
        const response = await axios.post('/evaluate_formula_view', { formula_id: formulaId, variables });
        setFormulaResult(response.data.result);
    };
    return (
        <div>
            <h1>Document Summarizer and Formula Builder</h1>
            <input type="file" multiple onChange={uploadDocuments} />
            <button onClick={() => generateSummary(1)}>Generate Summary</button>
            <p>Summary: {summary}</p>
            <button onClick={() => evaluateFormula(1, { x: 10, y: 5 })}>Evaluate Formula</button>
            <p>Formula Result: {formulaResult}</p>
        </div>
    );
}
export default App;
```

'''
Main entry point for the Django application.
'''
import os
import sys

os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'myproject.settings')

views.py
```python
'''
Django views for handling document uploads and formula operations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt
from .models import Document, Formula
from .nlp_utils import summarize_text
from .formula_utils import evaluate_formula
import json
@csrf_exempt
def upload_documents(request):
    '''
    Handle document uploads and save them to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        files = request.FILES.getlist('documents')
        for file in files:
            content = file.read().decode('utf-8')
            Document.objects.create(title=file.name, content=content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Documents uploaded successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def generate_summary(request, document_id):
    '''
    Generate a summary for a specific document.
    '''
    try:
        document = Document.objects.get(id=document_id)
        summary = summarize_text(document.content)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'summary': summary})
    except Document.DoesNotExist:
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Document not found.'})
@csrf_exempt
def save_formula(request):
    '''
    Save a new formula to the database.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        name = data.get('name')
        expression = data.get('expression')
        Formula.objects.create(name=name, expression=expression)
        return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'message': 'Formula saved successfully.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
@csrf_exempt
def evaluate_formula_view(request):
    '''
    Evaluate a formula using provided variables.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        data = json.loads(request.body)
        formula_id = data.get('formula_id')
        variables = data.get('variables', {})
        try:
            formula = Formula.objects.get(id=formula_id)
            result = evaluate_formula(formula.expression, variables)
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'success', 'result': result})
        except Formula.DoesNotExist:
            return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Formula not found.'})
    return JsonResponse({'status': 'error', 'message': 'Invalid request method.'})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Django models for storing documents and formulas.
'''
from django.db import models
class Document(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    content = models.TextField()
class Formula(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    expression = models.TextField()
```

nlp_utils.py
```python
'''
NLP utilities for text summarization.
'''
import spacy
nlp = spacy.load("en_core_web_sm")
def summarize_text(text):
    '''
    Simple summarization logic.
    '''
    doc = nlp(text)
    summary = ' '.join([sent.text for sent in doc.sents][:3])  # Example: first 3 sentences
    return summary
```

formula_utils.py
```python
'''
Utilities for formula evaluation.
'''
from asteval import Interpreter
def evaluate_formula(expression, variables):
    '''
    Evaluate the formula using the provided variables.
    '''
    try:
        aeval = Interpreter()
        for key, value in variables.items():
            aeval.symtable[key] = value
        result = aeval(expression)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        return str(e)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
PyQt5 GUI implementation for the application.
'''
from PyQt5.QtWidgets import QMainWindow, QWidget, QVBoxLayout, QPushButton, QLabel, QFileDialog
class MainWindow(QMainWindow):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setWindowTitle("Document Summarizer and Formula Builder")
        self.setGeometry(100, 100, 800, 600)
        self.central_widget = QWidget()
        self.setCentralWidget(self.central_widget)
        self.layout = QVBoxLayout()
        self.central_widget.setLayout(self.layout)
        self.upload_button = QPushButton("Upload Documents")
        self.upload_button.clicked.connect(self.upload_documents)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.upload_button)
        self.summary_label = QLabel("Summary will appear here.")
        self.layout.addWidget(self.summary_label)
        self.formula_button = QPushButton("Evaluate Formula")
        self.formula_button.clicked.connect(self.evaluate_formula)
        self.layout.addWidget(self.formula_button)
    def upload_documents(self):
        '''
        Logic to handle document upload.
        '''
        file_dialog = QFileDialog()
        file_dialog.setFileMode(QFileDialog.ExistingFiles)
        file_dialog.setNameFilter("Text files (*.txt)")
        if file_dialog.exec_():
            file_names = file_dialog.selectedFiles()
            # Process files
            self.summary_label.setText("Documents uploaded.")
    def evaluate_formula(self):
        '''
        Logic to evaluate a formula.
        '''
        self.summary_label.setText("Formula evaluated.")

app.js
```js
'''
React component for the main application interface.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
function App() {
    const [documents, setDocuments] = useState([]);
    const [summary, setSummary] = useState('');
    const [formulaResult, setFormulaResult] = useState('');
    const uploadDocuments = async (event) => {
        const files = event.target.files;
        const formData = new FormData();
        for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
            formData.append('documents', files[i]);
        }
        const response = await axios.post('/upload_documents', formData);
        console.log(response.data.message);
    };
    const generateSummary = async (documentId) => {
        const response = await axios.get(`/generate_summary/${documentId}`);
        setSummary(response.data.summary);
    };
    const evaluateFormula = async (formulaId, variables) => {
        const response = await axios.post('/evaluate_formula_view', { formula_id: formulaId, variables });
        setFormulaResult(response.data.result);
    };
    return (
        <div>
            <h1>Document Summarizer and Formula Builder</h1>
            <input type="file" multiple onChange={uploadDocuments} />
            <button onClick={() => generateSummary(1)}>Generate Summary</button>
            <p>Summary: {summary}</p>
            <button onClick={() => evaluateFormula(1, { x: 10, y: 5 })}>Evaluate Formula</button>
            <p>Formula Result: {formulaResult}</p>
        </div>
    );
}
export default App;
```

# LangChain

Building applications with LLMs through composability

Looking for the JS/TS version? Check out LangChain.js.

**Production Support:** As you move your LangChains into production, we'd love to offer more comprehensive support.

Please fill out this form and we'll set up a dedicated support Slack channel.

## Quick Install

`pip install langchain`

or

`conda install langchain -c conda-forge`

## 🤔 What is this?

Large language models (LLMs) are emerging as a transformative technology, enabling developers to build applications that they previously could not. However, using these LLMs in isolation is often insufficient for creating a truly powerful app - the real power comes when you can combine them with other sources of computation or knowledge.

This library aims to assist in the development of those types of applications. Common examples of these applications include:

**❓ Question Answering over specific documents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: Question Answering over Notion Database

**🤖 Agents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: GPT+WolframAlpha

## 📖 Documentation

Please see [here](https://python.langchain.com) for full documentation on:

- Getting started (installation, setting up the environment, simple examples)

- How-To examples (demos, integrations, helper functions)

- Reference (full API docs)

- Resources (high-level explanation of core concepts)

# Document Summarizer and Formula Builder

A web application built with Python/Django and React that enables bulk upload of documents, generates concise summaries using NLP, and includes a flexible formula builder for financial calculations. Users can save and edit formulas.

## Main Features

- **Bulk Document Upload**: Upload multiple documents at once for processing.
- **NLP-based Summarization**: Generate concise summaries of uploaded documents using Natural Language Processing.
- **Flexible Formula Builder**: Create, save, and evaluate financial formulas with customizable variables.

## Installation Guide

### Prerequisites

- Python 3.x
- Node.js and npm
- Django
- React
- PyQt5 (for GUI)
- SpaCy (for NLP)
- asteval (for formula evaluation)

### Setting Up the Environment

1. **Clone the Repository**

   Clone the project repository to your local machine.

   ```bash
   git clone <repository-url>
   cd <repository-directory>
   ```

2. **Install Python Dependencies**

   Create a virtual environment and install the required Python packages.

   ```bash
   python -m venv venv
   source venv/bin/activate  # On Windows use `venv\Scripts\activate`
   pip install -r requirements.txt
   ```

3. **Install Node.js Dependencies**

   Navigate to the frontend directory and install the necessary Node.js packages.

   ```bash
   cd frontend
   npm install
   ```

4. **Download NLP Model**

   Download the SpaCy language model required for text summarization.

   ```bash
   python -m spacy download en_core_web_sm
   ```

## Running the Application

1. **Start the Django Backend**

   Navigate to the root directory of the project and run the Django server.

   ```bash
   python manage.py runserver
   ```

2. **Start the React Frontend**

   Open a new terminal, navigate to the frontend directory, and start the React development server.

   ```bash
   cd frontend
   npm start
   ```

3. **Access the Application**

   Open your web browser and go to `http://localhost:3000` to access the application interface.

## Using the Application

### Uploading Documents

- Click on the "Upload Documents" button.
- Select multiple text files from your local machine.
- The application will process and store the documents in the database.

### Generating Summaries

- After uploading, click on "Generate Summary" for a specific document.
- The summary will be displayed on the interface.

### Building and Evaluating Formulas

- Use the formula builder to create new formulas.
- Save formulas for future use.
- Evaluate formulas by providing necessary variables.

## Troubleshooting

- Ensure all dependencies are correctly installed.
- Check if the Django server and React server are running without errors.
- Verify that the correct SpaCy model is downloaded.

## Support

For further assistance, please contact our support team at support@chatdev.com.
